 Political background: In 1957, Paika Murmu won from this seat on a Congress ticket
 iske baad congress ke hi tikat par 1962, 1967 or 1971 kaa chunaav ishwar marandi jeetne main kaamyaab hue
 Janata Party's Anton Murmu won from this seat in 1977
 1980 main congress ne phir vaapasi kii or uske tikat par 1980 va 1984 kaa chunaav seth hembhram jeetne main kaamyaab hue
 For the first time in 1989, Jharkhand Mukti Morcha's Kula won this seat and Simon Marandi won the elections of 1989 and 1991 on his ticket
 1996 main congress ke thomas hansda jite
 For the first time in 1998, Kamal played on this seat and won Marandi in Mon on his ticket from here
 1999 main congress ke thomas hansda jite
 jmm's Hemlal Murmu won the 2004 elections
 2009 kaa chunaav bijepi ke devidhan besara jeetne main kaamyaab hue

 'hansi to fansi' kii kahani gumti he 'nikhil', yani siddharth malhotra tathaa 'karishma', yani adaa sharma ke ird-gird, jo na sirf ek-duusare se muhabbat karte hai, balki unki shaadi bhi tay ho chuki he
 
 
 Only then does Nikhil meet, 'karishma''s younger sister' Mita ', ie Parineeti Chopra, who lives away from her family, and whose name the family does not want to take, because people have moved her a bit' 'understand
 
 
 iske baad phir 'nikhil' or 'mita' kii mulaakaat kya 'turn or twist' laati he, yah jaanane ke liye aapako film dekhni padegi, lekin mujhe 'hansi to fansi' main kya acha laga, or kya bura, yah main bataaungaa
 
 
 The first thing is that 'hansi Toh Fansi' is a romantic comedy, and its script and screenplay are very beautifully composed, but at times it feels dragging a lighthearted film
 
 
 film main kairectorizeshan bhi behtareen tareeke se kiya gaya he, or har kirdaar ko badi safai se gadha gaya he, phir chaahe vah pariniti chopra kaa charitra ho, adaa sharma kaa ho, yaa manoj joshi kaa
 
 
 So, once again for casting, Full Marks casting director Mukesh Chhabra, who cast many actors who seem absolutely Taylor-made in their roles
 
 
 masalan, anil maange, jo 'nikhil', yani siddharth malhotra ke rishtedaar kii bhoomika main hai
 
 
 He not only makes you laugh, but looks different and more effective than the everyday faces of Hindi cinema
 
 
 ab baat abhinay kii
 
 
 Parineeti Chopra plays her character beautifully, and Siddharth Malhotra and Ada Sharma have also done justice to their characters
 
 
 yahaan manoj joshi kaa zikr karnaa behad zaruri he, jinhone pariniti ke pita ke kirdaar main hai
 
 
 She has given excellent performances in many scenes
 
 
 sharat saxena or baaki chote-chote kirdaar bhi asar chhodane main kaamyaab rahe hai 'hansi to fansi' main
 
 
 'hansi Toh Fansi' is a situational comedy that will make you smile from time to time, while some scenes will also moisten your eyes
 
 
 lekin mere liye kahani kaa jo mukhya dhaancha he, vahi kaam nahin karata, kyonki pichley kuch samay main ham aisi kai filmein dekh chuke hai, jahaan ek ladkaa or ladki ek-duusare se ishk karte hai, or baad main unhen ehsaas hota he ki yah unka sachcha pyaar nahin he, or vah koi or hi he, jiske saath ve khush rah paaenge
 
 
 So, this is why you get a sense of what the story of the film will be at the beginning of the film
 
 
 bas, script, mazaakia dialogs, rochak charitra aapako pakadakar rakhte hai or aapkaa manoranjan bhi karte hai
 
 
 But you don't feel like you saw anything new
 
 
 sangeet kii baat karen to gaanaa 'drama queen
 
 
 ' i liked it
 
 
 film kaa treetment kaaphi had tak vaastavik rakhaa gaya he, jo mujhe acha laga

 phir bhi nae nirdeshak kaa kaam acha he

 is baat kaa andaja isi baat se lagaaya ja saktaa he ki is seat se sabase zyada 11 aam chunaavon main congress ne jeet kaa paracham laharaaya he

 1982 main tidipi ke gathan ke baad 1984 main aam chunaav hue jisamen tidipi ke sansthaapak anti ramarao kii aandhi main yah seat bhi congress ke haanthon se nikal gai
